LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

       <span class="hero-arrow-path ml-1 size-3 motion-safe:animate-spin"></span></p></div><div class="flex-1"></div><button type="button" class="group self-start cursor-pointer" aria-label="close"><span class="hero-x-mark size-5 opacity-40 group-hover:opacity-70"></span></button></div></div></div>


LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

       Attempting to reconnect
       <span class="hero-arrow-path ml-1 size-3 motion-safe:animate-spin"></span></p></div><div class="flex-1"></div><button type="button" class="group self-start cursor-pointer" aria-label="close"><span class="hero-x-mark size-5 opacity-40 group-hover:opacity-70"></span></button></div></div>


LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

       <span class="hero-arrow-path ml-1 size-3 motion-safe:animate-spin"></span></p></div><div class="flex-1"></div><button type="button" class="group self-start cursor-pointer" aria-label="close"><span class="hero-x-mark size-5 opacity-40 group-hover:opacity-70"></span></button></div></div></div>


LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

       <span class="hero-arrow-path ml-1 size-3 motion-safe:animate-spin"></span></p></div><div class="flex-1"></div><button type="button" class="group self-start cursor-pointer" aria-label="close"><span class="hero-x-mark size-5 opacity-40 group-hover:opacity-70"></span></button></div></div>


LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

       <span class="hero-arrow-path ml-1 size-3 motion-safe:animate-spin"></span></p></div><div class="flex-1"></div><button type="button" class="group self-start cursor-pointer" aria-label="close"><span class="hero-x-mark size-5 opacity-40 group-hover:opacity-70"></span></button></div></div></div>


LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.

LiveView requires that all elements have unique ids, duplicate IDs will cause
undefined behavior at runtime, as DOM patching will not be able to target the correct
elements.

You can change this to raise and fail your test instead of warning
by passing `on_error: :raise` to `Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live/3` or
`Phoenix.LiveViewTest.live_isolated/3`.
